# Glimmerdeep Mire Microcontent Pack — Emberwild_DepthPack_GIGA_Part3_2025-12-24_MicroPOIs

600 micro-POIs designed to increase moment-to-moment density.

### Glimmerdeep Micro-POI 001: Chalkgate Tidepool
- **Vibe:** warmth where there shouldn't be any
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Silt-grit Lichen (ID 49749) — Gear Helm.
- **Node:** Frostworn Wanted Poster (ID 47189) — Gear Boots.
- **Node:** Frostworn Seed (ID 46254) — Material Resin.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Lantern Wraiths (fear, light-sensitive)
  - Rime Crows (blind, peck)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Follow the cant marks to a hidden cache.
  - Escort a cart through the area during a storm window.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

### Glimmerdeep Micro-POI 002: Rime-Needle Turn
- **Vibe:** fog that makes sounds closer than they are
- **Gameplay:** 1–2 pulls, a reason to stop, and a reason to leave.
- **Gather / Loot:**
- **Node:** Frostbriar Salve (ID 49021) — Material Ingot.
- **Node:** Warden's Bottle (ID 45326) — Material Timber.
- **Node:** Gutterborn Bandage Roll (ID 45785) — Consumable Food.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Dock Rats (bleed, swarm)
  - Bogleeches (slow, stacking debuff)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Follow the cant marks to a hidden cache.
  - Recover a dropped ledger page before dawn.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).

- **Node:** Pilgrim's Vial (ID 48514) — Curio Charm.
- **Node:** Amberwake Ration (ID 49494) — Trophy Claw.
- **Enemy Packs:**
  - Bogleeches (slow, stacking debuff)
  - Lantern Wraiths (fear, light-sensitive)
- **Quest Hooks:**
  - Recover a dropped ledger page before dawn.
  - Bring back a sample for an alchemist’s field kit.
- **In-World Drop:** a small readable that hints at the area.
- **Design Note:** add one interactable (rope, bell, cache, chalk mark).
